  <script type="text/javascript"><!--
    function CocheAll() {
      var lst = $('.case').map(function(){return $(this).val();}).get().join(',');
      Coche(lst,1);
    }
    function Coche(id,all) {
      $.ajax({
	url: "ajax/checkinstitution.php",
	type: "POST",
	data: "id=" + id + "&all=" + all,
	cache: false,
	success:function(msg){
	  $("#tools").html(msg);
	  if ( !id ) $('.case').prop("checked", false);
	  if ( all ) $('.case').prop("checked", true);
	},
	error:function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrows){	// PB AJAX
	  $.fancybox('<p>AJAX ERROR</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
	}
      }); 
    }
  //--></script>

function Connexion() {

	$.ajax({
		url: "ajax/login.php",
		type: "POST",
		data: "user=" + $('#user').val() + "&pass=" + $('#pass').val(),
		cache: false,
		success:function(msg){
			switch (msg) {
				case 'ABSENT':
					$.fancybox('<p>Login details missing</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
					break;
				case 'INCONNU':
					$.fancybox('<p>Login details not recognized</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
					break;
				case 'SUSPENDU':
					$.fancybox('<p>Sorry, your account has been temporarily suspended</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
					break;
				case 'OK':
					window.top.location.href = "home.php";
					break;
				default:
					if ( msg ) {
						/* $.fancybox('<p>Sorry, your account has expired - <a href="payment.php?id='+msg+'">Reactivate</a></p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true}); */
						$.fancybox('<p>Sorry, your account has expired - <a href="expired.php?id='+msg+'">Reactivate</a></p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
					} else {
						$.fancybox('<p>AJAX ERROR</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});	
					} 
			} 
		},
		error:function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrows){	// PB AJAX
			$.fancybox('<p>AJAX ERROR</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
		}
	});

}
//-->
</script>

</div>

   	function Valide() {
   		if ( !$("#Chp10").val() && !$("#Chp1").val() && !$("#search").val() && $('input[name=membre]:checked', '#qsearch').val() == 0 ) {
      	$.fancybox({

   		}
   		$('#fsearch').submit();
   	}
